             <div class="par parsys">
              <div class="reference2 reference parbase section">
               <div class="unstructuredpage page basicpage">
                <div class="par parsys">
                 <div class="reference2 reference parbase section">
                  <script>
                   // Allow for multiple search's to appear on the same page (only define once).
if (!loadedSearchScripts) {
    /** Contains the IDs of all of the Funnelback search-concierge scripts that must be externally loaded before adding concirege (autocomplete) to the page. */
    var prereqSearchScriptIds = ['concierge-deps-script'];
    /** Contains the loaded status of each of the external Funnelback search (async) scripts. */
    var loadedSearchScripts = {};
    prereqSearchScriptIds.forEach(function (searchScriptId) {
        loadedSearchScripts[searchScriptId] = false;
    });
}

/**
 * Registers an external Funnelback search script as loaded.
 * @param {string} searchScriptId The ID (without hastag) of the search script element.
 */
function registerSearchScriptLoad(searchScriptId) {
    loadedSearchScripts[searchScriptId] = true;
}

/**
 * Initializes and adds the custom search in both desktop and mobile views.
 * @param {string} targetSelector The selector indicating where to place the custom search.
 * @param {string} ariaLabel The aria-label attribute that should be applied to the search container with role="search".
 * @param {boolean} replaceTarget Set to true to replace the target element. Default is false for place the custom search inside the target.
 * @param {boolean} isMenu Set to true to include the search inside a dropdown menu. The default is false for directly exposing the search form.
 */
function addCustomSearch(targetSelector, ariaLabel, replaceTarget, isMenu) {
    var searchMenu = compileSearchMenuTemplate();
    var searchForm = searchMenu.find('.form');
    var searchContainer = searchMenu.find('.search-container');
    var searchInput = searchContainer.find('.search-input');
    var searchSubmit = searchContainer.find('.search-submit');
    var isMobile = (jQuery(window).width() <= 720);

    if (isMenu) {
        // Add search menu & form.
        searchMenu.mouseenter(showSearchForm);
        searchMenu.mouseleave(hideSearchForm);
        searchMenu.focus(focusSearchInput);
        searchInput.focus(onSearchInputFocus);
        searchInput.blur(hideSearchForm);
        searchSubmit.blur(hideSearchForm);
        addOrReplaceSearch(searchMenu);
        searchMenu.removeClass('hide-until-ready');
        jQuery(window).resize(resizeSearchForm);
    } else {
        // Only add search form.
        addOrReplaceSearch(searchForm);
    }
    searchContainer.attr('aria-label', ariaLabel);
    addConciergeAfterAllScriptsLoaded();

    /**
     * Performs 'compilation' of the search menu template by transforming HTML text grabbed from
     * a script tag containing non-rendered HTML into child nodes of a dynamically created HTML Element.
     * @return The search menu HTML Element that has been 'compiled' from its text HTML template.
     */
    function compileSearchMenuTemplate() {
        var searchMenuHtml = jQuery('.search-menu-tmpl').first().html();
        var searchMenuTempContainer = jQuery(document.createElement('span'));
        searchMenuTempContainer.html(searchMenuHtml);
        searchMenu = searchMenuTempContainer.find('.search-menu');
        return searchMenu;
    }

    /**
     * Adds a search form or menu to the DOM. Will either add it by prepending it to the children of a target element,
     * or by replacing the target element based off of the 'replaceTarget' input value to the 'addCustomSearch' function.
     * @param {jQuery} search The search form or menu.
     */
    function addOrReplaceSearch(search) {
        var target = jQuery(targetSelector);
        (replaceTarget)
            ? target.replaceWith(search)
            : target.prepend(search);
    }

    function focusSearchInput() {
        showSearchForm();
        searchInput.focus();
    }

    function onSearchInputFocus() {
        searchInput.select();
    }

    function showSearchForm() {
        resizeSearchForm();
        searchMenu.addClass('show');
        searchMenu.attr('tabindex', -1);
    }

    function hideSearchForm() {
        // Only hide search form when a form element is not focused.
        setTimeout(function() {
            if ($(document.activeElement).parents('.search-menu').length === 0) {
                searchMenu.removeClass('show');
                searchMenu.attr('tabindex', 0);
            }
        });
    }

    function resizeSearchForm() {
        var xOffset = -searchMenu.offset().left;
        var bodyWidth = jQuery('body').width();
        var width = (bodyWidth < 960 && bodyWidth > 720) ? 960 : bodyWidth;
        searchForm.css('left', xOffset);
        searchForm.css('width', width);
    }

    /**
     * Waits until all external Funnelback scripts are loaded before proceeding with the addition of search concierge (autocomplete).
     */
    function addConciergeAfterAllScriptsLoaded() {
        if (areAllPrereqScriptsLoaded()) {
            // If all 3 prerequisite scripts have loaded before we reached this call to 'addCustomSearch', then add concierge immediately.
            addSearchConcierge();
        } else {
            // Else, listen for all pre-requisite scripts to load (NOTE: a subset may have loaded already).
            prereqSearchScriptIds.forEach(function(searchScriptId) {
                var prereqScript = jQuery('#' + searchScriptId);
                prereqScript.on('load', function() {
                    onPrereqScriptLoad(searchScriptId);
                });
            });
        }
    }

    /**
     * Whether or not all prerequisite Funnelback search (async) scripts have loaded.
     * @return true if they have all loaded, false if not.
     */
    function areAllPrereqScriptsLoaded() {
        var allLoaded = true;
        prereqSearchScriptIds.forEach(function(searchScriptId) {
            allLoaded = (allLoaded && loadedSearchScripts[searchScriptId]);
        });
        return allLoaded;
    }

    /**
     * Callback that fires whenever a prerequisite script loads. Increments the number of prereq scripts that have loaded,
     * and proceeds with the remainder of the script if all of them have loaded.
     */
    function onPrereqScriptLoad(searchScriptId) {
        loadedSearchScripts[searchScriptId] = true;
        if (areAllPrereqScriptsLoaded()) {
            addSearchConcierge();
        }
    }

    /**
     * Executes the actual add search operation after all prerequisite Funnelback search (async) scripts have loaded.
     */
    function addSearchConcierge() {
        // Associate concierge (auto-complete) with search input.
        searchInput.qc({
            datasets: {
                organic: {
                name: 'Suggestions',
                show: (isMobile) ? '8' : '12',
                profile: '_default',
                collection: 'meta-search',
                program: 'https://search.buffalo.edu/s/suggest.json',
                callback: function(set, suggestions) {
                    if (isMenu) {
                        jQuery('.tt-dataset-people')[0].style.width = (suggestions.length ? '50%' : '100%');
                    }
                    return suggestions;
                }
                },
                people: {
                name: 'People',
                show: (isMobile) ? '3' : '4',
                profile: 'autocompletion',
                collection: 'db-people',
                program: 'https://search.buffalo.edu/s/suggest.json',
                template: {
                    suggestion: jQuery('.auto-completion-people').text()
                },
                callback: function(set, suggestions) {
                    if (isMenu) {
                        jQuery('.tt-dataset-organic')[0].style.width = (suggestions.length ? '50%' : '100%');
                    }
                    for (var i = 0; i < suggestions.length; i++) {
                        var pathStartIdx = suggestions[i].extra.action.indexOf('/s/');
                        var newUrl = 'https://search.buffalo.edu' + suggestions[i].extra.action.substring(pathStartIdx);
                        suggestions[i].extra.action = newUrl;
                    }
                    return suggestions;
                }
                }
            }
        });
    }
}
                  </script>
                 </div>

  .eub-home .page .page-inner header .innerheader .tlw-header-title-inner .mobile-header-icon > a {

}

               <script>
                /**
 * Gets the duration of animations within the custom TLW header.
 * @return {number} The animation duration in milliseconds.
 */
function getTlwHeaderAnimationDuration() {
    var header = jQuery('header .innerheader .tlw-mobile-nav');
    var animationDuration = 200; // Default to 200 in case we cannot get duration from .innerheader CSS style.
    var headerTransition = header.css('transition');
    if (headerTransition) {
        var headerTransitionParts = headerTransition.split(' ');
        if (headerTransitionParts.length > 1) {
            var headerTransitionDuration = headerTransitionParts[1];
            animationDuration = parseFloat(headerTransitionDuration) * 1000;
        }
    }
    return animationDuration;
}
               </script>

              <div class="reference2 reference parbase section">
               <script>
                // Do NOT edit for content changes. This file contains functionality that is used to build & insert the TLW Rollover Nav Menus.

/**
 * Builds and inserts a custom TLW Rollover Navigation Menu.
 * @param {RolloverConfig} rolloverConfig The build configuration for the custom TLW rollover menu.
 * @param {RolloverConfig} fallbackConfig The build configuration to fallback to after a given date.
 */
function initCustomTlwRollover(rolloverConfig, fallbackConfig) {
    checkRequiredFields(rolloverConfig, fallbackConfig);
    rolloverConfig = chooseConfig(rolloverConfig, fallbackConfig);
    var topnavTmplId = (rolloverConfig.tmplId ? rolloverConfig.tmplId : '#tlw-jumbo-tmpl');
    var topnavTmpl = jQuery(topnavTmplId);
    var customTopnav = genCustomTopnav(topnavTmpl, rolloverConfig.index);

    customTopnav.addClass(rolloverConfig.customClass);
    prepareRolloverTitle(customTopnav, rolloverConfig);
    prepareRolloverImg(customTopnav, rolloverConfig);
    prepareRolloverDescription(customTopnav, rolloverConfig);
    insertAllColumnsAndLinks(customTopnav, rolloverConfig);
    moveRolloverImgDescriptionIfConfigRight(customTopnav, rolloverConfig);
    insertResources(customTopnav, rolloverConfig);
    markActiveLinks(customTopnav);
	removeHoverOnBlur(customTopnav);
    customTopnav.removeClass('hide-until-ready');

    function checkRequiredFields(rolloverConfig, fallbackConfig) {
        if (rolloverConfig.index == null) {
            alert('"index" field is missing on TLW Rollover rolloverConfig');
            throw new Error('"index" field is missing on TLW Rollover rolloverConfig');
        }
        if (rolloverConfig.title == null) {
            alert('"title" field is missing on TLW Rollover rolloverConfig');
			throw new Error('"title" field is missing on TLW Rollover rolloverConfig');
        }
        if (fallbackConfig) {
            if (fallbackConfig.index == null) {
                fallbackConfig.index = rolloverConfig.index;
            }
            if (fallbackConfig.title == null) {
                fallbackConfig.title = rolloverConfig.title;
            }
            if (!fallbackConfig.fallbackDate) {
                alert('"fallbackDate" is missing on TLW Rollover fallbackConfig');
                throw new Error('"fallbackDate" is missing on TLW Rollover fallbackConfig');
            }
            if (typeof fallbackConfig.fallbackDate === 'string') {
                fallbackConfig.fallbackDate = new Date(fallbackConfig.fallbackDate);
            }
        }
    }

    function chooseConfig(rolloverConfig, fallbackConfig) {
        return (fallbackConfig && fallbackConfig.fallbackDate <= new Date())
            ? fallbackConfig
            : rolloverConfig;
    }

    function genCustomTopnav(topnavTmpl, index) {
        var customTopnav = topnavTmpl.clone().attr('id', '');
        var topnavMenuItems = jQuery('.topnav .main > ul > li');
        if (topnavMenuItems[index]) {
            var tlwRolloverId = ('tlw-rollover-' + index);
            var topnavMenuItem = jQuery(topnavMenuItems[index]);
            topnavMenuItem.find('> a').attr('id', tlwRolloverId);
            topnavMenuItem.find('.topnav-submenu-container').remove();
            topnavMenuItem.append(customTopnav).attr('aria-labelledby', tlwRolloverId);
        }
        return customTopnav;
    }

    function prepareRolloverTitle(customTopnav, rolloverConfig) {
        var titleDiv = customTopnav.find('.rollover-title');
        if (typeof rolloverConfig.title === 'string') {
            titleDiv.text(rolloverConfig.title);
        } else if (rolloverConfig.title) {
            titleDiv.text(rolloverConfig.title.text);
            titleDiv.parent().attr('href', rolloverConfig.title.href);
        }
    }

    function prepareRolloverImg(customTopnav, rolloverConfig) {
        if (rolloverConfig.image) {
            var rolloverImgA = customTopnav.find('.rollover-img');
            var rolloverImg = rolloverImgA.find('img');
            rolloverImgA.css('background', 'url(' + rolloverConfig.image.url + ')');
            rolloverImgA.attr('href', rolloverConfig.image.href);
            rolloverImg.attr('src', rolloverConfig.image.url);
            rolloverImg.attr('alt', rolloverConfig.image.alt);
            rolloverImgA.removeClass('hide-until-ready');
        }
    }

    function prepareRolloverDescription(customTopnav, rolloverConfig) {
        var descriptionP = customTopnav.find('.rollover-description');
        if (typeof rolloverConfig.description === 'string') {
            descriptionP.text(rolloverConfig.description);
        } else if (rolloverConfig.description) {
            var descriptionTitleA = customTopnav.find('.rollover-description-title a');
            var descriptionA = customTopnav.find('.rollover-description-link a');
            var descriptionSpan = descriptionA.find('span');
            if (typeof rolloverConfig.description.title === 'string') {
                descriptionTitleA.text(rolloverConfig.description.title);
            } else if (rolloverConfig.description.title) {
                descriptionTitleA.text(rolloverConfig.description.title.text);
                descriptionTitleA.attr('href', rolloverConfig.description.title.href);
                descriptionTitleA.parent().removeClass('hide-until-ready');
            }
            descriptionP.text(rolloverConfig.description.text);
            if (rolloverConfig.description.link) {
                descriptionSpan.text(rolloverConfig.description.link.text);
                descriptionA.attr('href', rolloverConfig.description.link.href);
                descriptionA.parent().removeClass('hide-until-ready');
            }
        }
    }

    function insertAllColumnsAndLinks(customTopnav, rolloverConfig) {
        if (rolloverConfig.columns) {
            var columnUl = customTopnav.find('.rollover-column-list');
            var columnTmpl = customTopnav.find('.rollover-column-tmpl');
            for (var i = 0; i < rolloverConfig.columns.length; i++) {
                var column = rolloverConfig.columns[i];
                var columnLi = columnTmpl.clone().removeClass('rollover-column-tmpl').addClass('rollover-column');
                var columnLinkUl = columnLi.find('.link-list');
                columnLi.find('.rollover-column-title').text(column.title);
                insertColumnLinks(columnLinkUl, column.links);
                columnUl.append(columnLi);
            }
            columnTmpl.detach();
        }
    }

    function insertColumnLinks(columnLinkUl, links) {
        for (var i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
            var link = links[i];
            var linkLi = jQuery(document.createElement('li'));
            var linkA = jQuery(document.createElement('a')).addClass('rollover-cta');
            var linkSpan = jQuery(document.createElement('span'));
            var linkP = jQuery(document.createElement('p')).addClass('link-description');
            linkSpan.text(link.text);
            linkA.append(linkSpan);
            linkA.attr('href', link.href);
            linkLi.append(linkA);
            linkP.text(link.description);
            linkLi.append(linkP);
            columnLinkUl.append(linkLi);
        }
    }

    function moveRolloverImgDescriptionIfConfigRight(customTopnav, rolloverConfig) {
        if (rolloverConfig.customClass && rolloverConfig.customClass.indexOf('right') >= 0) {
            var columnUl = customTopnav.find('.rollover-column-list');
            var rolloverImgDescriptionRight = jQuery(document.createElement('li'));
            rolloverImgDescriptionRight.addClass('rollover-img-description-right');
            var rolloverImgDescriptionLeft = customTopnav.find('.rollover-img-description');
            var rolloverImgDescriptionContent = rolloverImgDescriptionLeft.find('> *').detach();
            rolloverImgDescriptionRight.append(rolloverImgDescriptionContent);
            columnUl.append(rolloverImgDescriptionRight);
        }
    }

    function insertResources(customTopnav, rolloverConfig) {
        if (rolloverConfig.resources || rolloverConfig.resourcesBar) {
            var resourceUl = customTopnav.find('.resources-bar ul');
            var resourcesBar = rolloverConfig.resourcesBar;
            var resources = (rolloverConfig.resources) ? rolloverConfig.resources : resourcesBar.resources;
            if (resourcesBar) {
                customTopnav.find('.resources-title-desktop').text(resourcesBar.title);
                customTopnav.find('.resources-title-mobile').text(resourcesBar.mobileTitle);
            }
            var topnavTitle = (typeof rolloverConfig.title === 'string') ? rolloverConfig.title : rolloverConfig.title.text;
            customTopnav.find('.resources-title-mobile').find('.ada-hidden').text(topnavTitle + ' resources that ');
            for (var i = 0; i < resources.length; i++) {
                var resource = resources[i];
                var resourceLi = jQuery(document.createElement('li'));
                var resourceA = jQuery(document.createElement('a')).addClass('rollover-cta');
                var resourceSpan = jQuery(document.createElement('span'));
                resourceSpan.text(resource.text);
                resourceA.append(resourceSpan);
                resourceA.attr('href', resource.href);
                resourceLi.append(resourceA);
                resourceUl.append(resourceLi);
            }
        }
    }

    function markActiveLinks(customTopnav) {
        customTopnav.find('a:not([href^="#"])').each(function() {
            if (this.href === window.location.href) {
                jQuery(this).addClass('active');
            }
        });
    }

    function removeHoverOnBlur(customTopnav) {
        var parentMenuLi = customTopnav.closest('ul.menu > li');
        parentMenuLi.find('a').on('blur', function() {
            setTimeout(function() {
                if (!parentMenuLi.find(document.activeElement).length) {
                    parentMenuLi.removeClass('hover');
                }
            });
        });
    }
}
               </script>
              </div>
              <div class="reference2 reference parbase section">
               <script>
                // Do NOT edit for content changes. This file contains functionality that is used to build & insert the TLW Rollover Mobile Menu.

/**
 * Builds and inserts all custom TLW Rollover Mobile Menus.
 */
function initCustomTlwMobileNav() {
    // Insert custom TLW Mobile Menu and setup its collapsible feature.
    var mobileNav = $('#tlw-mobile-nav');
    var collapsibleToggleIdCnt = 1;

    setupCollapsible(mobileNav, false, mobileNavToggleCollapible);
    setupBackdropClickListener();
    setupMobileNavScrollListener();
    transformDesktopNavMenusToMobile();
    addButtonFocusMasks();
    addAudienceNav();
    addTaskNav();
    addSocialNav();
    removeHoverOnBlur();
    addCustomMobileNavToHeader();
    jQuery('.header').remove(); // Remove old mobile header.

    // Remove empty TLW mobile menu slot template.
    mobileNav.find('.tlw-mobile-nav-slot').detach();

    /**
     * For each of the (desktop) topnav menu items, auto-construct a mobile version & insert into main mobile navigation menu.
     */
    function transformDesktopNavMenusToMobile() {
        var topnavMenuItems = $('header .innerheader .topnav .main > ul > li');
        topnavMenuItems.each(function(i, menuItem) {
            var menuItemAnchor = $(menuItem).find('> a');
            var menuItemTitle = $(menuItemAnchor).find('> span').text();
            var customTopnav = $(menuItem).find('> div.tlw-jumbo');
            var mobileNavSlot;
            if (customTopnav[0] && !customTopnav[0].classList.contains('no-tlw-mobile')) {
                mobileNavSlot = makeCustomTopnavMobileVersion(customTopnav, menuItemTitle, i);
            } else {
                mobileNavSlot = makeStandardTopNavMobileVersion(menuItemAnchor);
            }
            mobileNav.find('> div > ul').append(mobileNavSlot);
        });
    }

    /**
     * Generates mobile slot for each custom topnav rollover.
     * @param {jQuery} customTopnavMenu The desktop version of the custom TLW topnav rollover menu.
     * @param {string} menuItemTitle The title for the custom TLW topnav rollover.
     * @param {number} i The index of the custom topnav rollover.
     * @return {jQuery} The custom mobile menu slot.
     */
    function makeCustomTopnavMobileVersion(customTopnavMenu, menuItemTitle, i) {
        // Insert into mobile submenu.
        var customMobileNavSlot = $('.tlw-mobile-nav-slot').clone();
        var mobileCustomTopnavMenu = customTopnavMenu.clone();
        mobileCustomTopnavMenu.attr('id', 'tlw-mobile-rollover-' + (i + 1));
        mobileCustomTopnavMenu.addClass('tlw-mobile');
        customMobileNavSlot.removeClass('tlw-mobile-nav-slot');
        customMobileNavSlot.find('.collapsible-toggle .collapsible-toggle-title').text(menuItemTitle);
        customMobileNavSlot.find('.collapsible-content').append(mobileCustomTopnavMenu);
        setupCollapsible(customMobileNavSlot);

        // Setup all child collapsibles within each TLW rollover menu.
        mobileCustomTopnavMenu.find('.collapsible-container').each(function(i, collapsible) {
            setupCollapsible(collapsible, true);
        });

        return customMobileNavSlot;
    }

    /**
     * Sets up a collapsible toggle button and associated content.
     * @param {jQuery} collapsible The collapsible container (contains collapsible toggle and content).
     * @param {boolean} initOpen Whether or not to initialize the collapsible as open. Default is false.
     * @param {Function} toggleCollapsibleFn An optional function to replace the default toggle collapsible functionality.
     */
    function setupCollapsible(collapsible, initOpen, toggleCollapsibleFn) {
        var collapsibleToggle = $(collapsible).find('> .collapsible-toggle');
        var collapsibleContent = $(collapsible).find('> .collapsible-content');
        toggleCollapsibleFn = (toggleCollapsibleFn) ? toggleCollapsibleFn : defaultToggleCollapsible;
        collapsibleToggle.click(function() {
            toggleCollapsibleFn(collapsible, collapsibleToggle, collapsibleContent);
        });
        collapsibleToggle.on('keypress', function(e) {
            if (e.which === 13) {
                toggleCollapsibleFn(collapsible, collapsibleToggle, collapsibleContent);
            }
        });
        collapsibleToggle.attr('tabindex', '0');
        collapsibleToggle.attr('role', 'button');
        collapsibleToggle.attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
        collapsibleToggle.attr('aria-haspopup', 'true');
        collapsibleToggle.addClass('collapsible-title small');
        if (!collapsibleToggle.attr('id')) {
            collapsibleToggle.attr('id', 'mobile-collapsible-toggle-' + (++collapsibleToggleIdCnt))
        }
        collapsibleContent.hide();
        collapsibleContent.attr('role', 'region');
        collapsibleContent.attr('aria-labelledby', collapsibleToggle.attr('id'));
        if (initOpen) {
            toggleCollapsibleFn(collapsible, collapsibleToggle, collapsibleContent);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Toggles a given collapsible.
     * @param {jQuery} collapsible The collapsible container.
     * @param {jQuery} collapsibleToggle The collapsible toggle.
     * @param {jQuery} collapsibleContent The collapsible content.
     */
    function defaultToggleCollapsible(collapsible, collapsibleToggle, collapsibleContent) {
        $(collapsible).toggleClass('expanded');
        var expanded = ($(collapsible).hasClass('expanded') ? 'true' : 'false');
        collapsibleContent.slideToggle('fast');
        collapsibleToggle.attr('aria-expanded', expanded);
    }

    /**
     * Toggles the main mobile navigation menu. Slides the nav in from the right instead of using default vertical collapsible animation.
     * @param {jQuery} mobileNavContainer The mobile nav container.
     * @param {jQuery} mobileNavToggle The mobile nav toggle button.
     * @param {jQuery} mobileNavContent The content/drawer of the mobile nav.
     */
    function mobileNavToggleCollapible(mobileNavContainer, mobileNavToggle, mobileNavContent) {
        var header = $('header .innerheader');
        var titleInner = $('header .innerheader .tlw-header-title .tlw-header-title-inner');
        mobileNavContainer.toggleClass('expanded');
        mobileNavContent.show();
        var expanded = mobileNavContainer.hasClass('expanded') ? 'true' : 'false'
        if (!header.hasClass('full-height')) {
            header.addClass('full-height');
        } else {
            // Delay removal of full height until mobile nav menu is fully animated away.
            var animationDuration = getTlwHeaderAnimationDuration();
            setTimeout(function() {
                header.removeClass('full-height');
                mobileNavContent.hide();
            }, animationDuration);
        }
        titleInner.toggleClass('mobile-cover-ribbon');
        mobileNavToggle.attr('aria-expanded', expanded);
        $('html').toggleClass('disable-scroll');
    }

    /**
     * Sets up the click listener on the mobile nav backdrop. Closes the mobile menu when clicked.
     */
    function setupBackdropClickListener() {
        var backdrop = mobileNav.find('.mobile-nav-backdrop');
        var mobileNavToggle = $('.mobile-nav-toggle');
        backdrop.click(function() {
            mobileNavToggle.click();
        });
    }

    /**
     * Sets up a scroll listen for the mobile nav content/drawer.
     * When the content is scrolled down, a border will appear at the top of the mobile nav menu.
     */
    function setupMobileNavScrollListener() {
        var mobileNavDrawer = mobileNav.find('.mobile-nav-drawer');
        var mobileNavToggle = mobileNav.find('.mobile-nav-toggle');
        mobileNavDrawer.scroll(function() {
            if (mobileNavDrawer.scrollTop() === 0 && mobileNavToggle.hasClass('mobile-nav-scrolled-down')) {
                mobileNavToggle.removeClass('mobile-nav-scrolled-down');
            } else if (mobileNavDrawer.scrollTop() > 0 && !mobileNavToggle.hasClass('mobile-nav-scrolled-down')) {
                mobileNavToggle.addClass('mobile-nav-scrolled-down');
            }
        });
    }

    /**
     * Generates mobile slot for each standard (anchor) topnav.
     * @param {jQuery} menuItemAnchor The original standard menu item anchor.
     * @return {jQuery} The new standard menu item anchor.
     */
    function makeStandardTopNavMobileVersion(menuItemAnchor) {
        var customMobileNavSlot = $('.tlw-mobile-nav-slot').clone();
        var customMobileNavAnchor = menuItemAnchor.clone();
        customMobileNavSlot.removeClass('tlw-mobile-nav-slot');
        customMobileNavSlot.removeClass('collapsible-container');
        customMobileNavSlot.empty();
        customMobileNavAnchor.removeAttr('aria-haspopup');
        customMobileNavSlot.append(customMobileNavAnchor);
        customMobileNavAnchor.attr('id', 'tlw-mobile-' + customMobileNavAnchor.attr('id'));
        return customMobileNavSlot;
    }

    /**
     * Add focus masks to all buttons to prevent outline on click focus (only allow outline on tab focus).
     */
    function addButtonFocusMasks() {
        mobileNav.find('.collapsible-content .collapsible-toggle.submenu-heading').each(function(i, submenuToggle) {
            if (!$(submenuToggle).find('.focus-mask')[0]) {
                $(submenuToggle).attr('role', 'button');
                $(submenuToggle).attr('tabindex', '0');
                $(submenuToggle).append('<div class="focus-mask" tabindex="-1"></div>');
            }
        });
    }

    /**
     * Adds the audience (info for) nav to the given mobile menu.
     */
    function addAudienceNav() {
        var mobileNavContent = mobileNav.find('> .collapsible-content');
        var audienceNavWrapper = $('.audiencenav-wrapper')[0];
        if (audienceNavWrapper) {
            var audienceNavWrapper = $(audienceNavWrapper).clone();
            audienceNavWrapper.attr('tabindex', -1);
            var audienceNavLabel = audienceNavWrapper.find('.label');
            audienceNavLabel.addClass('collapsible-toggle');
            var audienceNavContent = audienceNavWrapper.find('ul');
            audienceNavContent.addClass('collapsible-content');
            setupCollapsible(audienceNavWrapper);
            mobileNavContent.append(audienceNavWrapper);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Adds the task nav to the given mobile menu.
     */
    function addTaskNav() {
        var mobileNavContent = mobileNav.find('> .collapsible-content');
        var taskNav = $('.tasknav')[0];
        if (taskNav) {
            mobileNavContent.append(taskNav);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Adds the social nav to the given mobile menu.
     * @param {jQuery} mobileNav The mobile menu.
     */
    function addSocialNav() {
        var mobileNavContent = mobileNav.find('> .collapsible-content');
        var socialNav = $('.social')[0];
        if (socialNav) {
            mobileNavContent.append(socialNav);
        }
    }

    /**
     * Adds the top level mobile menu toggle to the mobile header.
     */
    function addCustomMobileNavToHeader() {
        var mobileNavToggle = mobileNav.find('> .collapsible-toggle');
        mobileNavToggle.detach();
        $('.headerconfigpage.contentpage.page > .par.parsys').append(mobileNavToggle);
        $('.headerconfigpage.contentpage.page > .par.parsys').append(mobileNav);
        mobileNav.removeClass('hide-until-ready');
        mobileNavToggle.removeClass('hide-until-ready');
    }

    function removeHoverOnBlur() {
        var mobileNavContent = mobileNav.find('> .collapsible-content');
        mobileNavContent.find('a,input,button').on('blur', function() {
            setTimeout(function() {
                if (!mobileNavContent.find(document.activeElement).length && mobileNav.hasClass('expanded')) {
                    $('.mobile-nav-toggle').click();
                }
            });
        });
    }
}
               </script>
              </div>
              <div class="reference2 reference parbase section">
               <script>
                // Do NOT edit for content changes. This file contains functionality that is used to initialize the sticky funcitonality for the header/topnav.

/**
 * Sets up the sticky header functionality.
 */
function initStickyHeaderFunctionality() {
    var header = jQuery('header .innerheader');
    var topnavRibbon = header.find('.header-ribbon');
    var topnavRibbonHeight = (topnavRibbon.height() + 10) // (+10) Account for bottom :after part.
    var scrollThreshold = (topnavRibbonHeight + 80); // (+80) Give a bit of space before transition.
    var immediateRemoveStickyThreshold = 6;
    var removeStickyTimeout = null;
    var stickyAnimationInterval = null;
    header.addClass('animated');
    initStickyScrollListener();

    function initStickyScrollListener() {
        jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
            var scrollPos = $(window).scrollTop();
            var hasShowClass = header.hasClass('show');
            var hasStickyClass = header.hasClass('sticky');
            if (scrollPos >= scrollThreshold && !hasShowClass) {
                animatedAddSticky();
            } else if (scrollPos <= immediateRemoveStickyThreshold && hasStickyClass) {
                immediateRemoveSticky();
            } else if (scrollPos < scrollThreshold && hasShowClass) {
                animatedRemoveSticky();
            }
        });
    }

    function animatedAddSticky() {
        clearStickyTimers(); // Make sure we clear remove sticky timeout if quikcly scrolling back down again to sticky.
        header.removeClass('animated');
        header.removeClass('show');
        header.addClass('sticky');
        setTimeout(function() {
            header.addClass('animated');
            header.addClass('show');
        });
    }

    function immediateRemoveSticky() {
        clearStickyTimers();
        header.removeClass('show');
        header.removeClass('sticky');
    }

    function animatedRemoveSticky() {
        clearStickyTimers();
        header.removeClass('show');
        removeStickyAfterAnimation();
        // Monitor sticky header position relative to top of document so we can cancel animation if needed.
        monitorStickyHitDocumentTop();
    }

    function removeStickyAfterAnimation() {
        var animationDuration = getTlwHeaderAnimationDuration();
        removeStickyTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
            clearStickyTimers();
            header.removeClass('sticky');
        }, animationDuration);
    }

    function monitorStickyHitDocumentTop() {
        stickyAnimationInterval = setInterval(function() {
            var top = header.offset().top;
            if (top <= immediateRemoveStickyThreshold) {
                immediateRemoveSticky();
            }
        }, 5);
    }

    function clearStickyTimers() {
        clearInterval(stickyAnimationInterval);
        clearTimeout(removeStickyTimeout);
    }
}
               </script>
              </div>
              <div class="reference2 reference parbase section">

                /**
 * Edit this file to make content changes. Each custom rollover nav is built and inserted via invoking the "initCustomTlwRollover" function.
 * Each function call is given a TopnavConfig object, which specifies how to build and where to place the rollover navigation menu.
 *
 *
 * -- Required Fields --
 *
 * index: The zero-based index that the rollover nav menu will be placed at in the original navigation menu.
 *
 *
 * -- Optional Fields --
 * 
 * tmplId: Set this to a custom template's ID in order to provide a custom HTML template. You can fully build a custom template this way only using HTML,
 * and ignore all other fields.
 *
 * customClass: Set any one of these classes on a rollover config object's "customClass" field, and the rollover will take on the associated layout/styling.
 * There are currently 4 custom classes: 'tlw-rollover-2-col', 'tlw-rollover-no-img', 'tlw-rollover-description-above', 'tlw-rollover-img-description-right'
 *
 * title: Can either be a string or an object containing the title "text" and "href" fields.
 *
 * description: Can either be a string or an object containing title (optional), text (required), and link (optional) fields.
 *
 * image: An object that contains the image "url" (required), "href" (required), and "alt" (required) text fields.
 *
 * columns: An array/list containing objects that specify the (link) columns that are present in the nav menu. Each column object contains "title" (optional),
 * "links" (required), "description" (optional) fields.
 *
 * resources: An array/list containing objects that define the resource links for the menu. If this field is used, then don't use the "resourcesBar" field.
 *
 * resourcesBar: An object that contains a "title" (optional), "mobileTitle" (optional), and "resources" (required) fields. Used as an alternative to the
 * "resources" field described above in order to modify the title text of the resources bar.
 */

               <script>
                // Do NOT edit for content changes. This file contains functionality that is to initialize the TLW desktop & mobile headers.

(function initCustomTlwHeader() {
    jQuery('#tlw-jumbo-tmpl').remove();
    insertTitleIntoHeader();
    fixJaggedTitleRibbonSafari();
    insertApplyGiveButtonsIntoTopnav();
    initCustomTlwMobileNav();
    insertSearchFieldIntoHeader();
    initStickyHeaderFunctionality();

    function insertTitleIntoHeader() {
        var eubHome = jQuery('.eub-home');
        var topnav = jQuery('.topnav');
        var titleInner = jQuery('.tlw-header-title-inner');
        // Prevent duplicate h1 on page. Any page other than eub homepage will have its own h1.
        var title = (eubHome.length > 0)
            ? jQuery(document.createElement('h1'))
            : jQuery(document.createElement('div'));
        title.attr('class', 'tlw-header-title');
        title.prepend(titleInner);
        topnav.before(title);
        titleInner.removeClass('hide-until-ready');
    }

    function fixJaggedTitleRibbonSafari() {
        var header = jQuery('header .innerheader');
		if (
            navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Safari') != -1 &&
            navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Chrome') == -1 &&
            navigator.userAgent.indexOf('CriOS/') == -1
        ) {
            header.find('.header-ribbon .ribbon-bottom').addClass('safari-fix-jagged-borders');
        }
    }

    function insertApplyGiveButtonsIntoTopnav() {
        var topnavApplyGive = jQuery('.topnav-apply-give');
        var topnavRight = jQuery('.topnav .right');
        topnavRight.append(topnavApplyGive);
        topnavApplyGive.removeClass('hide-until-ready');
    }

    function insertSearchFieldIntoHeader() {
        addCustomSearch('header .innerheader .search', 'Main search', true, true);
        addCustomSearch('#tlw-mobile-nav .mobile-nav-drawer', 'Mobile search');
    }
})();
               </script>

    $(document).ready(function () {
        var isPlaying = true;
        $('.toggle-playback').on('click', function () {
            var togglePlaybackButton = $('.hero-video-wrapper .active')[0];

            var playPauseIcon = $('.hero-video-wrapper .toggle-playback i');
            playPauseIcon.toggleClass('icon-play3');
            playPauseIcon.toggleClass('icon-pause2');

            if (isPlaying) {
                togglePlaybackButton.pause();
                isPlaying = false;
            } else {
                togglePlaybackButton.play();
                isPlaying = true;
            }
        })

    })

                    return false
                });

                jQuery('#ubcms\u002Dgen\u002D13408877 .flexmodule-style.flexmodule-style-largeimg').each(function (indx) {
                    var $this = jQuery(this);
                    $this.removeClass('slides-hidden');
                    jQuery(this).on('focus', '*', function (e) {
                        slider.goToSlide(indx);
                        $this.closest("div.lSSlideWrapper").scrollLeft(0);
                    });
                })
            });
               </script>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>

               <script type="application/javascript">
                (function() {
        var undergraduateProgramSearchTab = jQuery('#tab-undergraduate');
        var undergraduateProgramSearchTabPanel = jQuery('#tab-panel-undergraduate');

        var graduateProgramSearchTab = jQuery('#tab-graduate');
        var graduateProgramSearchTabPanel = jQuery('#tab-panel-graduate');

        var activeTabClass = 'active';
        var inactiveTabClass = 'inactive';

        undergraduateProgramSearchTab.click(switchToUndergraduate);
        undergraduateProgramSearchTab.keypress(clickOnEnter);

        graduateProgramSearchTab.click(switchToGraduate);
        graduateProgramSearchTab.keypress(clickOnEnter);

        function switchToUndergraduate() {
            graduateProgramSearchTab.parent().removeClass(activeTabClass).addClass(inactiveTabClass);
            graduateProgramSearchTabPanel.hide();
            undergraduateProgramSearchTab.parent().removeClass(inactiveTabClass).addClass(activeTabClass);
            undergraduateProgramSearchTabPanel.show();
        }

        function switchToGraduate() {
            undergraduateProgramSearchTab.parent().removeClass(activeTabClass).addClass(inactiveTabClass);
            undergraduateProgramSearchTabPanel.hide();
            graduateProgramSearchTab.parent().removeClass(inactiveTabClass).addClass(activeTabClass);
            graduateProgramSearchTabPanel.show();
        }

        function clickOnEnter(event) {
            if (event.which === 13) {
                event.target.click();
            }
        }
    })();
               </script>

         <script>
          function moveCode() {    
    var codeToMove = document.getElementById('campaign-banner');
   
    var codeContainer = document.createElement('div');
    codeContainer.appendChild(codeToMove);
    
	var footerDiv = document.getElementsByClassName('footer-mode-fat');        
    
    var newDiv = footerDiv[0];
        
	newDiv.insertBefore(codeContainer, newDiv.childNodes[2]);
   
}

moveCode();
         </script>
